        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap">
            <p>
                <span>    The show follows first responders (Police, Fire, and EMS) in New Orleans working the night shift 2000 hours - 0400 hours. Cameras follow firefighters to their calls, EMS to patients' homes or whatever situation they may be called to, as well as Police chases or patrols.</span>
            </p>
        </div>

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                <span>
                    <strong>Nightwatch is Fantastic Show</strong>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        3 January 2016 | by <a href="/user/ur37095196/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span>lizzyblueyez</span></a>
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur37095196/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p>I absolutely LOVE this show it&#39;s kind of like COPS but it follows a group of EMS workers in &quot;The Big Easy&quot; or New Orleans. I like how they are all like a big close family.They really love their jobs and always have the other&#39;s back. Some of their reactions to situations are hilarious and you never know what&#39;s gonna come out their mouths. One thing I have to warn is that scenes can get kind of gory. On some of the calls, if you&#39;re queasy you WILL have to turn your face away from the TV. But thank God some of the more grotesque injuries are blurred out from the network.I always like how at the end of the show there are good updates for the people they treated.</p>
                    </div>
                </span>
